             var results = [];&amp;#x000A;              query = query.toLowerCase();&amp;#x000A;              for (i = 0; i &amp;lt; search_index.length; i++) {&amp;#x000A;                      if (search_index[i].method.indexOf(query) != -1) {&amp;#x000A;      function buildHtmlForResults(results) {&amp;#x000A;              var html = &amp;quot;&amp;quot;;&amp;#x000A;              var i;&amp;#x000A;              for (i = 0; i &amp;lt; results.length; i++) {&amp;#x000A;      }&amp;#x000A;&amp;#x000A;      function performSearch() {&amp;#x000A;              var query = $F(&amp;#39;search&amp;#39;);&amp;#x000A;              if (query == &amp;#39;&amp;#39;) {&amp;#x000A;
